***докатиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:докатиться.html>докати́ться</a> (14337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катиться.html>кати́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:докатиться.html>докати́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dokatítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дока́тываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll <i>(to)</i>, to go rolling <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to reach</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(sounds)</i> to roll, to thunder, to boom</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come down <i>(to)</i>, to sink <i>(into)</i>, to end up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:докатиться.html>докати́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:преступление.html>преступле́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dokatítʹsja</b> do prestuplénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sink into crime</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:докатиться.html>докати́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тюрьмы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dokatítʹsja</b> do tjurʹmy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to end up in jail</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:докатиться.html>докати́лся</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vot do čevó on <b>dokatílsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">that's what he has come down to!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***доклад.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доклад.html>докла́д</a> (2477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доклад.html>докла́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doklád</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доклад.html>докла́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доклад.html>докла́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доклад.html>докла́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>report, paper</li>
<li>lecture</li>
<li>announcement</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщение.html>сообще́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">soobščénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выступление.html>выступле́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vystuplénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лекция.html>ле́кция</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lékcija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчет.html>отчёт</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otčót</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кладывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kladyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:докладывать.html>докла́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dokládyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доложить.html>доложи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to report, to announce <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to notify formally</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to add more, to put more (e.g. into a portion)</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доколе.html>доко́ле</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dokóle</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> how long?</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> as long as, until</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:докопаться.html>докопа́ться</a> (18336)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">докопа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dokopátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:докопаться.html>докопа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dokopátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дока́пываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dig down <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <i>(try to)</i> find out, to discover, to hunt out, to arrive, to get to the bottom <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:докопаться.html>докопа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:суть.html>су́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dokopátʹsja</b> do súti dela</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get at the heart of the matter; get at the roots of things</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">докапывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dokapyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***доктор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доктор.html>до́ктор</a> (651)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доктор.html>до́ктор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dóktor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доктор.html>до́ктора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доктор.html>доктора́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доктор.html>докторо́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:докторша.html>до́кторша</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>doctor <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">PhD or MD</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доктор.html>до́ктор</a></b> жива́го</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Dóktor</b> Živágo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Doctor Zhivago</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Grammatically the word is a masculine, but it is used to refer to both a man and a woman and it is declinable in both cases. The term <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:докторша.html>до́кторша</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dóktorša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is also used for a woman in colloquial Russian, but it is nonstandard.</li></ul>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:докторский.html>до́кторский</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dóktorskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul></div><div class="list-switcher-element" data-showtext=" show more ▼ " data-hidetext=" show less  " style="display: none;"> </div></div>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долбать.html>долба́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dolbátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ану́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>

***долбать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:долбать.html>долба́ть</a> (26501)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dъlbati</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">довба́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dovbáty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">долбі́ць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dolbícʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ду̑псти</i> / <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">dȗpsti</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">dɫubać</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***долбить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:долбить.html>долби́ть</a> (9148)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dъlbiti</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">довба́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dovbáty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">долбі́ць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dolbícʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ду̑псти</i> / <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">dȗpsti</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">dłubać</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долбить.html>долби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dolbítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">продолби́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to peck (e.g. of birds), to gouge a hole in <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to make a dent or a hole by constantly hitting the surface</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>дя́тел</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:долбить.html>долби́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́реву</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Djátel <b>dolbít</b> po dérevu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The woodpecker pecks the wood.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to knock, to hit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to constantly repeat, to remind about something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:долбить.html>долби́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ет</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Skólʹko jemú ni <b>dolbí</b>, on étovo ne ponimájet.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He doesn't understand no matter how many times I repeat this.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to memorize by constantly repeating
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часа́ми</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:долбить.html>долби́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:урок.html>уро́к</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On časámi <b>dolbít</b> urók.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He does the exercise for hours by repeating over and over again.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scold, to criticize</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to destroy by using sloppily</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to use drugs</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fuck</li></ol>

***долгий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>до́лгий</a> (820)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьlgъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dl̥h₁gʰós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>до́лгий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dólgij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)до́льше</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)до́лее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:доля.html>до́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>long
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dólgo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for a long time</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
